var isJobSeeker = "";
var isLoggedIn = "";

document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
    if (!isLoggedIn && !isJobSeeker) {
        $('#navbar-main-content').on('show.bs.dropdown', function () {
            if (typeof mixpanel !== 'undefined') {
                mixpanel.track('Nav - Burger Menu - Opened');
            }
        });
    }

    $('#desktop-jobseeker-dropdown-menu').on('show.bs.dropdown', function () {
        $(this).find('.icon-burger-menu-container-mobile').addClass('active');
        if (typeof mixpanel !== 'undefined') {
            mixpanel.track('Nav - Burger Menu - Opened');
        }
    });

    $('#desktop-jobseeker-dropdown-menu').on('hide.bs.dropdown', function () {
        $(this).find('.icon-burger-menu-container-mobile').removeClass('active');
    });

    var variations = ['v1', 'v2', 'v3'];

    window.Wuzzuf = window.Wuzzuf || {};
    window.Wuzzuf.mobileGuestRandomNavigationVariation = variations[Math.floor(Math.random() * variations.length)];
    $('.full-screen-menu-container').addClass(Wuzzuf.mobileGuestRandomNavigationVariation);
}, false);

        var windowHeight = $(window).height();

        //////////////// Mega Menu ////////////////
        // If Mega menu height is more than the height of screen
        // 1- Enabling scrolling inside it
        // 2- blocking scrolling on the body
        // 3- Bluring backgeround in case of transperant navbar

        $(".browse-jobs-mega-menu").on('show.bs.dropdown', function(e){
            // $('.above-the-fold').addClass('bluring');
            if($('.mega-menu').height() > windowHeight-62){
                $('.mega-menu').addClass('mega-menu-scrolling');
                $('body').addClass('no-scrolling');
            }
        });

        $(".browse-jobs-mega-menu").on('hide.bs.dropdown', function(e){
            $('.mega-menu').removeClass('mega-menu-scrolling');
            $('body').removeClass('no-scrolling');
            // $('.above-the-fold').removeClass('bluring');
        });
        //////////////// Mobile Burger Menu ////////////////
        $('.main-burger-menu').click(function(e) {

            var onTop = !!$('.navbar.navbar-default.navbar-main.main-header.navbar-transparent').length;
            var onHomePage = !!$('body.wuzzuf-homepage').length;

            var headerClassName = onHomePage ? "navbar-transparent" : "navbar-fixed-top";

            if($('.main-menu').hasClass('show')) {
                $('body').removeClass('no-scrolling');
                $('.main-menu').removeClass('show');
                $('.icon-burger-menu-container-mobile').removeClass('active');
                // reset header position
                $('.navbar.navbar-main.main-header')
                    .removeClass('navbar-fixed-top before-appearing')
                    .addClass(headerClassName);
            } else {
                $('body').addClass('no-scrolling');
                $('.main-menu').addClass('show');
                var variationsNames = { v1: 'Bottom buttons', v2: 'Top buttons', v3: 'Icons' };
                mixpanel && mixpanel.track('Nav - Burger Menu - Opened', { Variation: variationsNames[window.Wuzzuf.mobileGuestRandomNavigationVariation] });
                $('.icon-burger-menu-container-mobile').addClass('active');
                if(onTop) {
                    $('.navbar.navbar-default.navbar-main.main-header.navbar-transparent')
                    .removeClass('navbar-transparent')
                    .addClass('before-appearing')
                    .addClass('navbar-fixed-top');
                }
            }
        });
        $('.close-menu').click(function(e) {
            $('.main-menu').css('display','none');
            $('body').removeClass('no-scrolling');
        });

        $('.user-menu-btn').click(function(e) {
            $('.user-menu').css('display','block');
            $('body').addClass('no-scrolling');
        });
        $('.close-menu').click(function(e) {
            $('.user-menu').css('display','none');
            $('body').removeClass('no-scrolling');
        });
